fmt.Sprintf(\"<error creating config string: %s>\", err)\n326: \t}\n327: \treturn string(b)\n328: }\n329: \n330: // GetScrapeConfigs returns the read-only, validated scrape configurations including\n331: // the ones from the scrape_config_files.\n332: // This method does not write to config, and it's concurrency safe (the pointer receiver is for efficiency).\n333: // This method also assumes the Config was created by Load or LoadFile function, it returns error\n334: // if it was not. We can't re-validate or apply globals here due to races,\n335: // read more https://github.com/prometheus/prometheus/issues/15538.\n336: func (c *Config) GetScrapeConfigs() ([]*ScrapeConfig, error) {\n337: \tif !c.loaded {\n338: \t\t// Programmatic error, we warn before more confusing errors would happen due to lack of the globalization.\n339: \t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"scrape config cannot be fetched, main config was not validated and loaded correctly; should not happen\")\n340: \t}\n341: \n342: \tscfgs := make([]*ScrapeConfig, len(c.ScrapeConfigs))\n343: \tjobNames := map[string]string{}\n344: \tfor i, scfg := range c.ScrapeConfigs {\n345: \t\tjobNames[scfg.JobName] = \"main config file\"\n346: \t\tscfgs[i] = scfg\n347: \t}\n348: \n349: \t// Re-read and validate the dynamic scrape config rules.\n350: \tfor _, pat := range c.ScrapeConfigFiles {\n351: \t\tfs, err := filepath.Glob(pat)\n352: \t\tif err != nil {\n353: \t\t\t// The only error can be a bad pattern.\n354: \t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"error retrieving scrape config files for %q: %w\", pat, err)\n355: \t\t}\n356: \t\tfor _, filename := range fs {\n357: \t\t\tcfg := ScrapeConfigs{}\n358: \t\t\tcontent, err := os.ReadFile(filename)\n359: \t\t\tif err != nil {\n360: \t\t\t\treturn nil, fileErr(filename, err)\n361: \t\t\t}\n362: \t\t\terr = yaml.UnmarshalStrict(content, &cfg)\n363: \t\t\tif err != nil {\n364: \t\t\t\treturn nil, fileErr(filename, err)\n365: \t\t\t}\n366: \t\t\tfor _, scfg := range cfg.ScrapeConfigs {\n367: \t\t\t\tif err := scfg.Validate(c.GlobalConfig); err != nil {\n368: \t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fileErr(filename, err)\n369: \t\t\t\t}\n370: \n371: \t\t\t\tif f, ok := jobNames[scfg.JobName]; ok {\n372: \t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fileErr(filename, fmt.Errorf(\"found multiple scrape configs with job name %q, first found in %s\", scfg.JobName, f))\n373: \t\t\t\t}\n374: \t\t\t\tjobNames[scfg.JobName] = fmt.Sprintf(\"%q\", filePath(filename))\n375: \n376: \t\t\t\tscfg.SetDirectory(filepath.Dir(filename))\n377: \t\t\t\tscfgs = append(scfgs, scfg)\n378: \t\t\t}\n379: \t\t}\n380: \t}\n381: \treturn scfgs, nil\n382: }\n383: \n384: // UnmarshalYAML implements the yaml.Unmarshaler interface.\n385: // NOTE: This method should not be used outside of this package. Use Load or LoadFile instead.\n386: func (c *Config) UnmarshalYAML(unmarshal func(any) error) error {\n387: \t*c = DefaultConfig\n388: \t// We want to set c to the defaults and then overwrite it with the input.\n389: \t// To make unmarshal fill the plain data struct rather than calling UnmarshalYAML\n390: \t// again, we have to hide it using a type indirection.\n391: \ttype plain Config\n392: \tif err := unmarshal((*plain)(c)); err != nil {\n393: \t\treturn err\n394: \t}\n395: \n396: \t// If a global block was open but empty the default global config is overwritten.\n397: \t// We have to restore it here.\n398: \tif c.GlobalConfig.isZero() {\n399: \t\tc.GlobalConfig = DefaultGlobalConfig\n400: \t}\n401: \n402: \t// If a runtime block was open but empty the default runtime config is overwritten.\n403: \t// We have to restore it here.\n404: \tif c.Runtime.isZero() {\n405: \t\tc.Runtime = DefaultRuntimeConfig\n406: \t}\n407: \n408: \tfor _, rf := range c.RuleFiles {\n409: \t\tif !patRulePath.MatchString(rf) {\n410: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid rule file path %q\", rf)\n411: \t\t}\n412: \t}\n413: \n414: \tfor _, sf := range c.ScrapeConfigFiles {\n415: \t\tif !patRulePath.MatchString(sf) {\n416: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid scrape config file path %q\", sf)\n417: \t\t}\n418: \t}\n419: \n420: \t// Do global overrides and validation.\n421: \tjobNames := map[string]struct{}{}\n422: \tfor _, scfg := range c.ScrapeConfigs {\n423: \t\tif err := scfg.Validate(c.GlobalConfig); err != nil {\n424: \t\t\treturn err\n425: \t\t}\n426: \t\tif _, ok := jobNames[scfg.JobName]; ok {\n427: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"found multiple scrape configs with job name %q\", scfg.JobName)\n428: \t\t}\n429: \t\tjobNames[scfg.JobName] = struct{}{}\n430: \t}\n431: \n432: \tif err := c.AlertingConfig.Validate(c.GlobalConfig.MetricNameValidationScheme); err != nil {\n433: \t\treturn err\n434: \t}\n435: \n436: \trwNames := map[string]struct{}{}\n437: \tfor _, rwcfg := range c.RemoteWriteConfigs {\n438: \t\tif rwcfg == nil {\n439: \t\t\treturn errors.New(\"empty or null remote write config section\")\n440: \t\t}\n441: \t\t// Skip empty names, we fill their name with their config hash in remote write code.\n442: \t\tif _, ok := rwNames[rwcfg.Name]; ok && rwcfg.Name != \"\" {\n443: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"found multiple remote write configs with job name %q\", rwcfg.Name)\n444: \t\t}\n445: \t\tif err := rwcfg.Validate(c.GlobalConfig.MetricNameValidationScheme); err != nil {\n446: \t\t\treturn err\n447: \t\t}\n448: \t\trwNames[rwcfg.Name] = struct{}{}\n449: \t}\n450: \trrNames := map[string]struct{}{}\n451: \tfor _, rrcfg := range c.RemoteReadConfigs {\n452: \t\tif rrcfg == nil {\n453: \t\t\treturn errors.New(\"empty or null remote read config section\")\n454: \t\t}\n455: \t\t// Skip empty names, we fill their name with their config hash in remote read code.\n456: \t\tif _, ok := rrNames[rrcfg.Name]; ok && rrcfg.Name != \"\" {\n457: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"found multiple remote read configs with job name %q\", rrcfg.Name)\n458: \t\t}\n459: \t\trrNames[rrcfg.Name] = struct{}{}\n460: \t}\n461: \treturn nil\n462: }\n463: \n464: // GlobalConfig configures values that are used across other configuration\n465: // objects.\n466: type GlobalConfig struct {\n467: \t// How frequently to scrape targets by default.\n468: \tScrapeInterval model.Duration `yaml:\"scrape_interval,omitempty\"`\n469: \t// The default timeout when scraping targets.\n470: \tScrapeTimeout model.Duration `yaml:\"scrape_timeout,omitempty\"`\n471: \t// The protocols to negotiate during a scrape. \n529: // Validate returns error if given scrape protocol is not supported.\n530: func (s ScrapeProtocol) Validate() error {\n531: \tif _, ok := ScrapeProtocolsHeaders[s]; !ok {\n532: \t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unknown scrape protocol %v, supported: %v\",\n533: \t\t\ts, func() (ret []string) {\n534: \t\t\t\tfor k := range ScrapeProtocolsHeaders {\n535: \t\t\t\t\tret = append(ret, a particular ScrapeProtocol.\n545: func (s ScrapeProtocol) HeaderMediaType() string {\n546: \tif _, ok := ScrapeProtocolsHeaders[s]; !ok {\n547: \t\treturn \"\"\n548: \t}\n549: \tmediaType, _, err := mime.ParseMediaType(ScrapeProtocolsHeaders[s])\n550: \tif err != nil {\n551: \t\treturn \"\"\n552: \t}\n553: \treturn mediaType\n554: }\n555: \n556: var (\n557: \tPrometheusProto      ScrapeProtocol = \"PrometheusProto\"\n558: \tPrometheusText0_0_4  ScrapeProtocol = \"PrometheusText0.0.4\"\n559: \tPrometheusText1_0_0  ScrapeProtocol = \"PrometheusText1.0.0\"\n560: \tOpenMetricsText0_0_1 ScrapeProtocol = \"OpenMetricsText0.0.1\"\n561: \tOpenMetricsText1_0_0 ScrapeProtocol = \"OpenMetricsText1.0.0\"\n562: \tUTF8NamesHeader      string         = model.EscapingKey + \"=\" + we see problems with accept scrape protocols option.\n595: func validateAcceptScrapeProtocols(sps []ScrapeProtocol) error {\n596: \tif len(sps) == 0 {\n597: \t\treturn errors.New(\"scrape_protocols cannot be empty\")\n598: \t}\n599: \tdups := map[string]struct{}{}\n600: \tfor _, sp := range sps {\n601: \t\tif _, ok := dups[strings.ToLower(string(sp))]; ok {\n602: \t\t\treturn }\n882: \n883: // Validate validates scrape config, but also fills relevant default values from global config if needed.\n884: func (c *ScrapeConfig) Validate(globalConfig GlobalConfig) error {\n885:
